   <div class="container PageMainContent Full" id="PageMainContent Page-1">
    <div class="row">
     <div class="col-sm-12">
      <img alt="Coddenham Parish Council" class="img-fluid" src="/assets/Uploads/Coddenham-Church.jpg"/>
      <div class="row">
       <div class="col-sm-12 col-xs-12 column col-md-12" style="">
        <div class="ge-content ge-content-type-ckeditor" data-ge-content-type="ckeditor">
         <p style="text-align:center">
          <span style="font-size:16px">
           <strong>
            Coddenham was the largest settlement in Suffolk during the Roman occupation of Britain.
           </strong>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align:center">
          <span style="font-size:16px">
           <strong>
            Situated on the B1078, 2 miles to the east of the A140 in the heart of Mid Suffolk, the village sits just eight miles to the north of the County Town of Ipswich.
           </strong>
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2 style="text-align:center">
          <span style="font-size:16px">
           <strong>
            Facilities include a village shop, country club and the community &amp; sports hall.
           </strong>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p style="text-align:center">
          <span style="font-size:16px">
           <strong>
            On this website you will find information about local events and services. Use the links at the top to find what you need.
           </strong>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align:center">
         </p>
         <p style="text-align:center">
          <span style="font-size:16px">
           <strong>
            This Website will focus on the formal business of the Parish Council.
           </strong>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align:center">
          <span style="font-size:16px">
           <strong>
            For a less formal look at life in the village of Coddenham please see the new
            <a href="http://coddenham.website">
             coddenham village website
            </a>
           </strong>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align:center">
          <span style="font-size:16px">
           <strong>
            Please check the News tag for important items affecting the Village
           </strong>
          </span>
         </p>
         <div>
          <p>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(function($) {
 
     checkCookie_eu();
 
     function checkCookie_eu()
     {
 
 
 
         var consent = getCookie_eu("cookies_consent");
 
         if (consent == null || consent == "" || consent == undefined)
         {
             // show notification bar
 
             $('#cookies_popup').show();
         }
 
     }
 
     function setCookie_eu(c_name,value,exdays)
     {
 
         var exdate = new Date();
         exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
         var c_value = escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString());
         document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value+"; path=/";
 
         $('#cookies_popup').hide('slow');
     }
 
 
 
     function getCookie_eu(cname) {
       var name = cname + "=";
       var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
       var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
       for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
           var c = ca[i];
           while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
               c = c.substring(1);
           }
           if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
               return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
           }
       }
       return "";
   }
 
     $("#close_cookies_popup").click(function(){
         setCookie_eu("cookies_consent", 1, 30);
     });
 
 });
   </script>
   <style type="text/css">
    div#cookies_popup{
   display: none;
         position: fixed;
     bottom: 0;
     background-color: black;
     color: white;
     width: 100%;
     padding: 5px 8%;
     font-size: 14px;
     font-weight: 500;
     z-index: 10000;
   }
   div#cookies_popup p{
     float: left;
     margin-bottom: 0px;
     padding-top: 3px;
   }
   div#cookies_popup button{
     float: right;
     color: white;
     background-color: red;
     margin-top: -5px;
     margin-bottom: -5px;
         border-radius: 0px;
     font-size: 13px;
     padding: 11px;
   }
   div#cookies_popup button:focus{
     box-shadow: 0px;
   }
   </style>
